Bed warmer: You don't sleep with it. As bed time is nigh, coals from the hearth are shoveled into the pan.  (It has a hinged lid.) Using the wood handle, the warmer is walked up to each bedroom.  The covers are raised on one side of the bed.  The hot pan is slipped between the covers and the mattress, and it is slid all over the mattress.  (Hence the long handle to reach all corners of the mattress.) Then the pan is removed and carried to the next bedroom....  So you never are in bed with brass pan.  It is too hot.  Instead it makes crawling into bed like putting on clothes straight out of the dryer.... FWIW.
